======================================================================
IOTASK STALE RELEASE CALLERS AUDIT
======================================================================

Goal:
  The release guard prevented final-destructor UAF, but the same 80-byte free cell later crashed in CreateQueuedCharacter.
  This audits release/set/get wrappers and caller contexts to find where stale task pointers are retained.
